}

country_event = { #Svetlana distinguishes herself as a valuable asset
	id = NIK.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event NIK.1"}
	title = NIK.1.t
	desc = NIK.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalina_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept her as an agent
		name = NIK.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NIK.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_med = yes
	}
	option = { #She cannot be trusted
		name = NIK.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NIK.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Voz cuts ties
	id = NIK.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event NIK.8"}
	title = NIK.8.t
	desc = NIK.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NIK.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NIKZhdanovFavors > 15 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.9
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NIKZhdanovFavors < 16 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.10
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = NIK_VOZNESENSKY_CUT_TIES
	}
}

country_event = { #Vote of no confidence
	id = NIK.25
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event NIK.25"}
	title = NIK.25.t
	desc = NIK.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_komi_government

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NIK.25.a
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {	NIKKosyginInfluence > NIKStalinaInfluence }
				check_variable = {	NIKKosyginInfluence > NIKVoznesenskyInfluence }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NIK.27
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = NIK.25.b
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {	NIKStalinaInfluence > NIKVoznesenskyInfluence }
				check_variable = {	NIKStalinaInfluence > NIKKosyginInfluence }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = NIK.28
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #The election process begins - violence at the polls
	id = NIK.172
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event NIK.172"}
	title = NIK.172.t
	desc = NIK.172.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_bobbies_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = NIK.172.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NIKCenterPower > NIKLeftPower }
					check_variable = { NIKCenterPower > NIKRightPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.173
					hours = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NIKCenterPower < NIKLeftPower }
					check_variable = { NIKLeftPower > NIKRightPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.174
					hours = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { NIKCenterPower < NIKRightPower }
					check_variable = { NIKRightPower > NIKLeftPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.175
					hours = 2
				}
				NIK_elect_the_president = yes
				set_variable = { NIKCoupRisk = 6 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = NIK.173
					hours = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = NIK.329.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIK_Voznesensky_Dead
				}

			custom_effect_tooltip = NIK_voznesensky_kill_tt
			set_country_flag = NIK_Voznesensky_Dead

			NIK_eliminate_center_leader = yes

				name = "National Assembly"
				desc = "POLITICS_NATIONAL_ASSEMBLY_DESC"

				expire = "1999.1.1"
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
				traits = {

				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIK_Kosygin_Dead
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = NIK_kosygin_kill_tt
			set_country_flag = NIK_Kosygin_Dead
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "National Assembly"
				desc = "POLITICS_NATIONAL_ASSEMBLY_DESC"
				picture = "Portrait_NIK_National_Assembly.dds"
				expire = "1999.1.1"

				}
			}
			set_variable = { NIKKosyginInfluence = 0 }
			NIK_decrease_center_power_high = yes
			NIK_eliminate_center_leader = yes
		}
		NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_high = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_high = yes
			NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_high = yes
			NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_high = yes
			NIK_increase_Stalina_influence_high = yes
		}
		NIK_decrease_coup_risk_med = yes
	}
}

		}

	id = komi_authdem.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event komi_authdem.1"}
	title = komi_authdem.1.t
	desc = komi_authdem.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_psd

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = komi_authdem.1.a
		NIK_PSD_empower_right_low = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				RUS_add_ruling_party_temp_pop_small = yes
				add_to_variable = { RUS_state_socdem_temp_pop = 0.015 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = komi_authdem.1.b
		NIK_PSD_empower_left_low = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				RUS_add_ruling_party_temp_pop_small = yes
				add_to_variable = { RUS_state_liberal_temp_pop = 0.015 }
			}
		}
	}
}
